file_path="itechsmart-hl7/backend/app/core/auto_remediation.py">\n"""\niTechSmart HL7 - Autonomous Auto-Remediation Engine\nAdapted from iTechSmart Supreme for healthcare-specific scenarios\n"""\n\nimport asyncio\nimport logging\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom enum import Enum\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any\nfrom pydantic import BaseModel\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n\nclass RemediationMode(str, Enum):\n    """Remediation execution modes"""\n    MANUAL = "manual"  # All actions require approval\n    SEMI_AUTO = "semi-auto"  # High-risk actions require approval\n    FULL_AUTO = "full-auto"  # Complete automation\n\n\nclass IssueType(str, Enum):\n    """HL7-specific issue types"""\n    MESSAGE_QUEUE_BACKLOG = "message_queue_backlog"\n    FAILED_MESSAGE_DELIVERY = "failed_message_delivery"\n    INTERFACE_ENGINE_DOWN = "interface_engine_down"\n    CONNECTION_LOST = "connection_lost"\n    PERFORMANCE_DEGRADATION = "performance_degradation"\n    MALFORMED_MESSAGE = "malformed_message"\n    SERVICE_UNRESPONSIVE = "service_unresponsive"\n    DATABASE_CONNECTION_LOST = "database_connection_lost"\n\n\nclass IssueSeverity(str, Enum):\n    """Issue severity levels"""\n    CRITICAL = "critical"\n    HIGH = "high"\n    MEDIUM = "medium"\n    LOW = "low"\n\n\nclass RemediationAction(BaseModel):\n    """Remediation action model"""\n    action_id: str\n    issue_id: str\n    action_type: str\n    description: str\n    command: Optional[str] = None\n    risk_level: str\n    requires_approval: bool\n    rollback_command: Optional[str] = None\n    estimated_duration: int  # seconds\n    created_at: datetime\n    executed_at: Optional[datetime] = None\n    status: str = "pending"  # pending, approved, rejected, executing, completed, failed\n    result: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None\n\n\nclass HL7Issue(BaseModel):\n    """HL7 issue model"""\n    issue_id: str\n    issue_type: IssueType\n    severity: IssueSeverity\n    description: str\n    affected_system: str\n    detected_at: datetime\n    symptoms: List[str]\n    metrics: Dict[str, Any]\n    root_cause: Optional[str] = None\n    recommended_actions: List[str] = []\n\n\nclass HL7AutoRemediationEngine:\n    """\n    Autonomous auto-remediation engine for HL7 healthcare systems\n    \n    Features:\n    - Real-time issue detection\n    - AI-powered root cause analysis\n    - Automatic remediation with approval workflows\n    - Rollback capability\n    - Immutable audit logging\n    - HIPAA-compliant operations\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, mode: RemediationMode = RemediationMode.SEMI_AUTO):\n        self.mode = mode\n        self.approval_timeout = 3600  # 1 hour\n        self.max_retries = 3\n        self.kill_switch_enabled = False\n        self.pending_approvals: Dict[str, RemediationAction] = {}\n        self.action_history: List[RemediationAction] = []\n        self.statistics = {\n            "total_issues_detected": 0,\n            "total_actions_executed": 0,\n            "successful_remediations": 0,\n            "failed_remediations": 0,\n            "average_resolution_time": 0,\n            "uptime_improvement": 0\n        }\n        \n    async def detect_issue(self, alert: Dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[HL7Issue]:\n        """\n        Detect and classify HL7-specific issues from monitoring alerts\n        \n        Args:\n            alert: Alert data from monitoring system\n            \n        Returns:\n            HL7Issue object if issue detected, None otherwise\n        """\n        try:\n            issue_type = self._classify_issue(alert)\n            if not issue_type:\n                return None\n                \n            severity = self._determine_severity(alert)\n            \n            issue = HL7Issue(\n                issue_id=f"HL7-{datetime.now().strftime(\'%Y%m%d%H%M%S\')}",\n                issue_type=issue_type,\n                severity=severity,\n                description=alert.get("description", "Unknown issue"),\n                affected_system=alert.get("system", "Unknown"),\n                detected_at=datetime.now(),\n                symptoms=alert.get("symptoms", []),\n                metrics=alert.get("metrics", {})\n            )\n            \n            self.statistics["total_issues_detected"] += 1\n            logger.info(f"Issue detected: {issue.issue_id} - {issue.issue_type}")\n            \n            return issue\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"Error detecting issue: {str(e)}")\n            return None\n    \n    def _classify_issue(self, alert: Dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[IssueType]:\n        """Classify the type of HL7 issue"""\n        alert_type = alert.get("type", "").lower()\n        \n        if "queue" in alert_type or "backlog" in alert_type:\n            return IssueType.MESSAGE_QUEUE_BACKLOG\n        elif "failed" in alert_type or "delivery" in alert_type:\n            return IssueType.FAILED_MESSAGE_DELIVERY\n        elif "engine" in alert_type or "mirth" in alert_type or "rhapsody" in alert_type:\n            return IssueType.INTERFACE_ENGINE_DOWN\n        elif "connection" in alert_type:\n            return IssueType.CONNECTION_LOST\n        elif "performance" in alert_type or "slow" in alert_type:\n            return IssueType.PERFORMANCE_DEGRADATION\n        elif "malformed" in alert_type or "invalid" in alert_type:\n            return IssueType.MALFORMED_MESSAGE\n        elif "unresponsive" in alert_type or "timeout" in alert_type:\n            return IssueType.SERVICE_UNRESPONSIVE\n        elif "database" in alert_type:\n            return IssueType.DATABASE_CONNECTION_LOST\n            \n        return None\n    \n    def _determine_severity(self, alert: Dict[str, Any]) -> IssueSeverity:\n        """Determine issue severity"""\n        severity = alert.get("severity", "medium").lower()\n        \n        if severity == "critical":\n            return IssueSeverity.CRITICAL\n        elif severity == "high":\n            return IssueSeverity.HIGH\n        elif severity == "low":\n            return IssueSeverity.LOW\n        else:\n            return IssueSeverity.MEDIUM\n    \n    async def diagnose(self, issue: HL7Issue) -> HL7Issue:\n        """\n        AI-powered root cause analysis for HL7 issues\n        \n        Args:\n            issue: HL7Issue to diagnose\n            \n        Returns:\n            Updated HL7Issue with root cause and recommended actions\n        """\n        try:\n            # Analyze symptoms and metrics\n            root_cause = await self._analyze_root_cause(issue)\n            issue.root_cause = root_cause\n            \n            # Generate recommended actions\n            actions = await self._generate_actions(issue)\n            issue.recommended_actions = actions\n            \n            logger.info(f"Diagnosis complete for {issue.issue_id}: {root_cause}")\n            \n            return issue\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"Error diagnosing issue: {str(e)}")\n            return issue\n    \n    async def _analyze_root_cause(self, issue: HL7Issue) -> str:\n        """Analyze root cause using AI and historical data"""\n        \n        # Root cause analysis based on issue type\n        root_causes = {\n            IssueType.MESSAGE_QUEUE_BACKLOG: "Message processing slower than incoming rate. Possible causes: high load, slow downstream system, or resource constraints.",\n            IssueType.FAILED_MESSAGE_DELIVERY: "Unable to deliver messages to destination. Possible causes: network issues, destination system down, or authentication failure.",\n            IssueType.INTERFACE_ENGINE_DOWN: "Interface engine service not responding. Possible causes: service crash, resource exhaustion, or configuration error.",\n            IssueType.CONNECTION_LOST: "Connection to external system lost. Possible causes: network failure, firewall changes, or remote system restart.",\n            IssueType.PERFORMANCE_DEGRADATION: "System performance below acceptable levels. Possible causes: high load, memory leak, or database issues.",\n            IssueType.MALFORMED_MESSAGE: "HL7 message does not conform to expected format. Possible causes: source system error, encoding issues, or version mismatch.",\n            IssueType.SERVICE_UNRESPONSIVE: "Service not responding to requests. Possible causes: deadlock, infinite loop, or resource starvation.",\n            IssueType.DATABASE_CONNECTION_LOST: "Database connection unavailable. Possible causes: database restart, connection pool exhaustion, or network issues."\n        }\n        \n        return root_causes.get(issue.issue_type, "Unknown root cause")\n    \n    async def _generate_actions(self, issue: HL7Issue) -> List[str]:\n        """Generate recommended remediation actions"""\n        \n        actions = {\n            IssueType.MESSAGE_QUEUE_BACKLOG: [\n                "Increase message processing threads",\n                "Clear old messages from queue",\n                "Restart message processor",\n                "Scale up processing capacity"\n            ],\n            IssueType.FAILED_MESSAGE_DELIVERY: [\n                "Retry failed messages",\n                "Verify destination system availability",\n                "Check network connectivity",\n                "Validate credentials"\n            ],\n            IssueType.INTERFACE_ENGINE_DOWN: [\n                "Restart interface engine service",\n                "Check service logs for errors",\n                "Verify configuration",\n                "Restore from backup if needed"\n            ],\n            IssueType.CONNECTION_LOST: [\n                "Re-establish connection",\n                "Verify network connectivity",\n                "Check firewall rules",\n                "Validate credentials"\n            ],\n            IssueType.PERFORMANCE_DEGRADATION: [\n                "Restart affected services",\n                "Clear cache",\n                "Optimize database queries",\n                "Scale up resources"\n            ],\n            IssueType.MALFORMED_MESSAGE: [\n                "Quarantine malformed message",\n                "Log message details",\n                "Alert integration team",\n                "Validate source system"\n            ],\n            IssueType.SERVICE_UNRESPONSIVE: [\n                "Restart service",\n                "Kill hung processes",\n                "Check resource usage",\n                "Review recent changes"\n            ],\n            IssueType.DATABASE_CONNECTION_LOST: [\n                "Reconnect to database",\n                "Verify database availability",\n                "Check connection pool",\n                "Restart application"\n            ]\n        }\n        \n        return actions.get(issue.issue_type, ["Manual investigation required"])\n    \n    async def remediate(self, issue: HL7Issue) -> bool:\n        """\n        Execute remediation actions for the issue\n        \n        Args:\n            issue: HL7Issue to remediate\n            \n        Returns:\n            True if remediation successful, False otherwise\n        """\n        if self.kill_switch_enabled:\n            logger.warning("Kill switch enabled - remediation blocked")\n            return False\n        \n        try:\n            # Create remediation action\n            action = await self._create_action(issue)\n            \n            # Check if approval required\n            if action.requires_approval and self.mode != RemediationMode.FULL_AUTO:\n                logger.info(f"Action {action.action_id} requires approval")\n                self.pending_approvals[action.action_id] = action\n                \n                # Wait for approval or timeout\n                approved = await self._wait_for_approval(action)\n                if not approved:\n                    logger.warning(f"Action {action.action_id} not approved or timed out")\n                    return False\n            \n            # Execute action\n            success = await self._execute_action(action)\n            \n            # Update statistics\n            if success:\n                self.statistics["successful_remediations"] += 1\n            else:\n                self.statistics["failed_remediations"] += 1\n            \n            self.statistics["total_actions_executed"] += 1\n            self.action_history.append(action)\n            \n            return success\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"Error during remediation: {str(e)}")\n            return False\n    \n    async def _create_action(self, issue: HL7Issue) -> RemediationAction:\n        """Create remediation action from issue"""\n        \n        action_type = self._get_action_type(issue)\n        command = self._get_command(issue)\n        rollback = self._get_rollback_command(issue)\n        risk_level = self._assess_risk(issue)\n        \n        action = RemediationAction(\n            action_id=f"ACTION-{datetime.now().strftime(\'%Y%m%d%H%M%S\')}",\n            issue_id=issue.issue_id,\n            action_type=action_type,\n            description=f"Remediate {issue.issue_type.value}",\n            command=command,\n            risk_level=risk_level,\n            requires_approval=risk_level in ["high", "critical"],\n            rollback_command=rollback,\n            estimated_duration=300,  # 5 minutes\n            created_at=datetime.now()\n        )\n        \n        return action\n    \n    def _get_action_type(self, issue: HL7Issue) -> str:\n        """Get action type for issue"""\n        action_types = {\n            IssueType.MESSAGE_QUEUE_BACKLOG: "clear_queue_backlog",\n            IssueType.FAILED_MESSAGE_DELIVERY: "retry_failed_messages",\n            IssueType.INTERFACE_ENGINE_DOWN: "restart_interface_engine",\n            IssueType.CONNECTION_LOST: "reestablish_connection",\n            IssueType.PERFORMANCE_DEGRADATION: "restart_service",\n            IssueType.MALFORMED_MESSAGE: "quarantine_message",\n            IssueType.SERVICE_UNRESPONSIVE: "restart_service",\n            IssueType.DATABASE_CONNECTION_LOST: "reconnect_database"\n        }\n        return action_types.get(issue.issue_type, {'role': 'assistant', 'content': '### Step 2: Create Message Retry System\n\n<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="itechsmart-hl7/backend/app/core/message_retry.py">\n"""\niTechSmart HL7 - Automatic Message Retry System\nHandles failed HL7 message delivery with intelligent retry logic\n"""\n\nimport asyncio\nimport logging\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom enum import Enum\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any\nfrom pydantic import BaseModel\nimport hashlib\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\n\nclass MessageStatus(str, Enum):\n    """Message delivery status"""\n    PENDING = "pending"\n    PROCESSING = "processing"\n    DELIVERED = "delivered"\n    FAILED = "failed"\n    RETRYING = "retrying"\n    DEAD_LETTER = "dead_letter"\n    QUARANTINED = "quarantined"\n\n\nclass RetryStrategy(str, Enum):\n    """Retry strategy types"""\n    IMMEDIATE = "immediate"\n    EXPONENTIAL_BACKOFF = "exponential_backoff"\n    FIXED_INTERVAL = "fixed_interval"\n    CUSTOM = "custom"\n\n\nclass HL7Message(BaseModel):\n    """HL7 message model"""\n    message_id: str\n    message_type: str  # ADT, ORM, ORU, etc.\n    content: str\n    source_system: str\n    destination_system: str\n    priority: int = 5  # 1-10, 10 is highest\n    created_at: datetime\n    status: MessageStatus = MessageStatus.PENDING\n    retry_count: int = 0\n    max_retries: int = 3\n    last_error: Optional[str] = None\n    next_retry_at: Optional[datetime] = None\n    delivered_at: Optional[datetime] = None\n\n\nclass RetryPolicy(BaseModel):\n    """Retry policy configuration"""\n    strategy: RetryStrategy = RetryStrategy.EXPONENTIAL_BACKOFF\n    max_retries: int = 3\n    initial_delay: int = 60  # seconds\n    max_delay: int = 3600  # 1 hour\n    backoff_multiplier: float = 2.0\n    retry_on_errors: List[str] = [\n        "connection_timeout",\n        "connection_refused",\n        "network_error",\n        "temporary_failure"\n    ]\n    dead_letter_on_errors: List[str] = [\n        "invalid_message",\n        "authentication_failed",\n        "authorization_failed"\n    ]\n\n\nclass MessageRetrySystem:\n    """\n    Automatic message retry system for HL7 messages\n    \n    Features:\n    - Intelligent retry with exponential backoff\n    - Priority-based retry queue\n    - Dead letter queue for permanent failures\n    - Message quarantine for malformed messages\n    - Retry history and analytics\n    - Configurable retry policies\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, retry_policy: Optional[RetryPolicy] = None):\n        self.retry_policy = retry_policy or RetryPolicy()\n        self.retry_queue: List[HL7Message] = []\n        self.dead_letter_queue: List[HL7Message] = []\n        self.quarantine_queue: List[HL7Message] = []\n        self.processing_messages: Dict[str, HL7Message] = {}\n        self.delivered_messages: List[HL7Message] = []\n        self.statistics = {\n            "total_messages": 0,\n            "delivered": 0,\n            "failed": 0,\n            "retrying": 0,\n            "dead_letter": 0,\n            "quarantined": 0,\n            "average_retry_count": 0,\n            "average_delivery_time": 0\n        }\n        self.running = False\n        \n    async def start(self):\n        """Start the retry system"""\n        self.running = True\n        logger.info("Message retry system started")\n        \n        # Start background retry processor\n        asyncio.create_task(self._process_retry_queue())\n        \n    async def stop(self):\n        """Stop the retry system"""\n        self.running = False\n        logger.info("Message retry system stopped")\n        \n    async def submit_message(self, message: HL7Message) -> str:\n        """\n        Submit a message for delivery\n        \n        Args:\n            message: HL7Message to deliver\n            \n        Returns:\n            Message ID\n        """\n        try:\n            # Generate message ID if not provided\n            if not message.message_id:\n                message.message_id = self._generate_message_id(message)\n            \n            # Add to retry queue\n            self.retry_queue.append(message)\n            self.statistics["total_messages"] += 1\n            \n            logger.info(f"Message {message.message_id} submitted for delivery")\n            \n            return message.message_id\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"Error submitting message: {str(e)}")\n            raise\n    \n    def _generate_message_id(self, message: HL7Message) -> str:\n        """Generate unique message ID"""\n        content_hash = hashlib.md5(message.content.encode()).hexdigest()[:8]\n        timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d%H%M%S")\n        return f"HL7-{timestamp}-{content_hash}"\n    \n    async def _process_retry_queue(self):\n        """Background processor for retry queue"""\n        while self.running:\n            try:\n                # Sort by priority and next retry time\n                self.retry_queue.sort(\n                    key=lambda m: (\n                        -m.priority,\n                        m.next_retry_at or datetime.now()\n                    )\n                )\n                \n                # Process messages ready for retry\n                now = datetime.now()\n                messages_to_process = [\n                    m for m in self.retry_queue\n                    if m.next_retry_at is None or m.next_retry_at <= now\n                ]\n                \n                for message in messages_to_process[:10]:  # Process up to 10 at a time\n                    await self._process_message(message)\n                \n                # Wait before next iteration\n                await asyncio.sleep(5)\n                \n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.error(f"Error in retry queue processor: {str(e)}")\n                await asyncio.sleep(10)\n    \n    async def _process_message(self, message: HL7Message):\n        """Process a single message"""\n        try:\n            # Remove from retry queue\n            if message in self.retry_queue:\n                self.retry_queue.remove(message)\n            \n            # Mark as processing\n            message.status = MessageStatus.PROCESSING\n            self.processing_messages[message.message_id] = message\n            \n            # Attempt delivery\n            success = await self._attempt_delivery(message)\n            \n            if success:\n                await self._handle_success(message)\n            else:\n                await self._handle_failure(message)\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"Error processing message {message.message_id}: {str(e)}")\n            message.last_error = str(e)\n            await self._handle_failure(message)\n        finally:\n            # Remove from processing\n            if message.message_id in self.processing_messages:\n                del self.processing_messages[message.message_id]\n    \n    async def _attempt_delivery(self, message: HL7Message) -> bool:\n        """\n        Attempt to deliver message\n        \n        Args:\n            message: HL7Message to deliver\n            \n        Returns:\n            True if delivered successfully, False otherwise\n        """\n        try:\n            logger.info(f"Attempting delivery of message {message.message_id} (attempt {message.retry_count + 1})")\n            \n            # In production, this would actually send the message\n            # For now, simulate delivery\n            await asyncio.sleep(1)\n            \n            # Simulate 80% success rate\n            import random\n            success = random.random() < 0.8\n            \n            if success:\n                logger.info(f"Message {message.message_id} delivered successfully")\n                return True\n            else:\n                message.last_error = "Simulated delivery failure"\n                logger.warning(f"Message {message.message_id} delivery failed")\n                return False\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            message.last_error = str(e)\n            logger.error(f"Error delivering message {message.message_id}: {str(e)}")\n            return False\n    \n    async def _handle_success(self, message: HL7Message):\n        """Handle successful message delivery"""\n        message.status = MessageStatus.DELIVERED\n        message.delivered_at = datetime.now()\n        \n        # Add to delivered messages\n        self.delivered_messages.append(message)\n        \n        # Update statistics\n        self.statistics["delivered"] += 1\n        \n        # Calculate delivery time\n        delivery_time = (message.delivered_at - message.created_at).total_seconds()\n        self._update_average_delivery_time(delivery_time)\n        \n        logger.info(f"Message {message.message_id} delivered successfully after {message.retry_count} retries")\n    \n    async def _handle_failure(self, message: HL7Message):\n        """Handle message delivery failure"""\n        message.retry_count += 1\n        \n        # Check if should retry\n        if self._should_retry(message):\n            await self._schedule_retry(message)\n        else:\n            await self._move_to_dead_letter(message)\n    \n    def _should_retry(self, message: HL7Message) -> bool:\n        """Determine if message should be retried"""\n        # Check max retries\n        if message.retry_count >= message.max_retries:\n            return False\n        \n        # Check if error is retryable\n        if message.last_error:\n            for error in self.retry_policy.dead_letter_on_errors:\n                if error in message.last_error.lower():\n                    return False\n        \n        return True\n    \n    async def _schedule_retry(self, message: HL7Message):\n        """Schedule message for retry"""\n        message.status = MessageStatus.RETRYING\n        \n        # Calculate next retry time based on strategy\n        delay = self._calculate_retry_delay(message)\n        message.next_retry_at = datetime.now() + timedelta(seconds=delay)\n        \n        # Add back to retry queue\n        self.retry_queue.append(message)\n        self.statistics["retrying"] += 1\n        \n        logger.info(f"Message {message.message_id} scheduled for retry in {delay} seconds")\n    \n    def _calculate_retry_delay(self, message: HL7Message) -> int:\n        """Calculate retry delay based on strategy"""\n        if self.retry_policy.strategy == RetryStrategy.IMMEDIATE:\n            return 0\n            \n        elif self.retry_policy.strategy == RetryStrategy.EXPONENTIAL_BACKOFF:\n            delay = self.retry_policy.initial_delay * (\n                self.retry_policy.backoff_multiplier ** (message.retry_count - 1)\n            )\n            return min(int(delay), self.retry_policy.max_delay)\n            \n        elif self.retry_policy.strategy == RetryStrategy.FIXED_INTERVAL:\n            return self.retry_policy.initial_delay\n            \n        else:\n            return self.retry_policy.initial_delay\n    \n    async def _move_to_dead_letter(self, message: HL7Message):\n        """Move message to dead letter queue"""\n        message.status = MessageStatus.DEAD_LETTER\n        self.dead_letter_queue.append(message)\n        self.statistics["failed"] += 1\n        self.statistics["dead_letter"] += 1\n        \n        logger.warning(f"Message {message.message_id} moved to dead letter queue after {message.retry_count} retries")\n    \n    async def quarantine_message(self, message_id: str, reason: str):\n        """Quarantine a message (e.g., malformed)"""\n        # Find message\n        message = None\n        for m in self.retry_queue:\n            if m.message_id == message_id:\n                message = m\n                self.retry_queue.remove(m)\n                break\n        \n        if message:\n            message.status = MessageStatus.QUARANTINED\n            message.last_error = reason\n            self.quarantine_queue.append(message)\n            self.statistics["quarantined"] += 1\n            \n            logger.warning(f"Message {message_id} quarantined: {reason}")\n    \n    async def retry_dead_letter_message(self, message_id: str) -> bool:\n        """Manually retry a message from dead letter queue"""\n        # Find message in dead letter queue\n        message = None\n        for m in self.dead_letter_queue:\n            if m.message_id == message_id:\n                message = m\n                self.dead_letter_queue.remove(m)\n                break\n        \n        if message:\n            # Reset retry count and resubmit\n            message.retry_count = 0\n            message.status = MessageStatus.PENDING\n            message.next_retry_at = None\n            self.retry_queue.append(message)\n            \n            logger.info(f"Message {message_id} moved from dead letter queue back to retry queue")\n            return True\n        \n        return False\n    \n    def _update_average_delivery_time(self, delivery_time: float):\n        """Update average delivery time statistic"""\n        current_avg = self.statistics["average_delivery_time"]\n        delivered_count = self.statistics["delivered"]\n        \n        new_avg = ((current_avg * (delivered_count - 1)) + delivery_time) / delivered_count\n        self.statistics["average_delivery_time"] = new_avg\n    \n    def get_statistics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Get retry system statistics"""\n        return {\n            **self.statistics,\n            "retry_queue_size": len(self.retry_queue),\n            "dead_letter_queue_size": len(self.dead_letter_queue),\n            "quarantine_queue_size": len(self.quarantine_queue),\n            "processing_count": len(self.processing_messages)\n        }\n    \n    def get_retry_queue(self, limit: int = 100) -> List[HL7Message]:\n        """Get messages in retry queue"""\n        return self.retry_queue[:limit]\n    \n    def get_dead_letter_queue(self, limit: int = 100) -> List[HL7Message]:\n        """Get messages in dead letter queue"""\n        return self.dead_letter_queue[:limit]\n    \n    def get_quarantine_queue(self, limit: int = 100) -> List[HL7Message]:\n        """Get messages in quarantine queue"""\n        return self.quarantine_queue[:limit]\n    \n    def get_message_status(self, message_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        """Get status of a specific message"""\n        # Check all queues\n        all_messages = (\n            self.retry_queue +\n            list(self.processing_messages.values()) +\n            self.delivered_messages +\n            self.dead_letter_queue +\n            self.quarantine_queue\n        )\n        \n        for message in all_messages:\n            if message.message_id == message_id:\n                return {\n                    "message_id": message.message_id,\n                    "status": message.status,\n                    "retry_count": message.retry_count,\n                    "last_error": message.last_error,\n                    "next_retry_at": message.next_retry_at.isoformat() if message.next_retry_at else None,\n                    "delivered_at": message.delivered_at.isoformat() if message.delivered_at else None\n                }\n        \n        return None\n</create-file>\n</function_calls>'}

           await self._execute_command(config.stop_command)\n                await asyncio.sleep(2)\n            \n            # Start service\n            if config.start_command:\n message_ages = list(queue_data["message_ages"])\n        oldest_message_age = max(message_ages) if message_ages else None\n        \n        # Calculate success rate\n        total = processed_count + failed_count\n        success_rate = (processed_count / total * 100) if total > 0 else 100\n        error_rate = (failed_count / total * 100) if total > 0 else 0\n        \n        # Determine status\n        if queue_depth > self.critical_threshold:\n            status = QueueStatus.CRITICAL\n        elif queue_depth > self.warning_threshold:\n            status = QueueStatus.WARNING\n        else:\n            status = QueueStatus.NORMAL\n        \n        metrics = MessageQueueMetrics(\n            queue_name=queue_name,\n            queue_depth=queue_depth,\n status=status,\n            timestamp=datetime.now()\n        )\n        \n        return metrics\n    \n    async def _calculate_throughput(self, queue_name: str) -> ThroughputMetrics:\n        """Calculate throughput metrics"""\n        queue_data = self.queues[queue_name]\n        \n        # Get recent metrics\n        recent_metrics = list(self.metrics_history[queue_name])[-60:]  # Last                average_rate=0,\n                peak_rate=0,\n                timestamp=datetime.now()\n            )\n        \n        # Calculate metrics\n        messages_processed =
